GT Equivalence Verification (PO34)
============================================================
GT: -c0*beta*v - mu*(c1 - v**c2)*v - omega0**c3*(gamma*Abs(v)**c4 + c5)*x
Candidate formulas: 50

Let the GT be rewritten in a simpler expanded form.

### Ground Truth (fixed)
GT:
\[
-0.721004421988058\,v(1-v^2)\;-\;1.03737009496134\,v\;-\;2.44077135428351\,x\,(0.0154128049692563|v|^{1/3}+1)
\]

Expand:
- First term: \(-0.7210\,v + 0.7210\,v^3\)
- Second term: \(-1.03737\,v\)
- Third term: \(-2.44077\,x - (2.44077\cdot 0.0154128)\,x|v|^{1/3}\)

So GT is exactly of the form:
\[
(0.7210044)\,v^3 \;+\;(-0.7210044-1.0373701)\,v \;+\;(-2.4407714)\,x \;+\;(-0.037616\ldots)\,x|v|^{1/3}
\]
and **nothing else** (no constants, no logs, no exp, no \(t\)-dependence, no \(v^2x\), etc.).

Numerically, the linear-in-\(v\) coefficient is:
\[
-0.721004421988058 - 1.03737009496134 = -1.758374516949398
\]
and the \(x|v|^{1/3}\) coefficient is:
\[
-2.44077135428351\cdot 0.0154128049692563 \approx -0.037616\ (\text{nonzero})
\]

So any matching candidate must be able to produce exactly:
- a \(v^3\) term,
- a \(v\) term,
- an \(x\) term,
- an \(x|v|^{1/3}\) term,
and must be able to set all other structures to zero.

Also, **the absolute value is essential**: \(x|v|^{1/3}\) cannot be replaced by \(xv^{1/3}\) globally because \(v\) can be negative.

---

## Candidate-by-candidate analysis

### 1
Has \(v^3, v, \text{constant }c2, x v^{c4}, x\log(1+c6|v|), x e^{c8|v|}, x\).
To match GT we must kill constant, log, exp: set \(c2=0, c5=0, c7=0\).
Then need \(x|v|^{1/3}\) but only has \(x v^{c4}\) (no Abs). Not globally equivalent. **No match**.

### 2
Has extra constant \(c9\) and also explicit \(+x\).
Can set \(c9=0\). The \(+x\) can be absorbed by choosing \(c8\) to make total \(x\) coefficient correct. But still only \(x v^{c3}\) (no Abs) and log/exp terms must be zeroed. Even after zeroing log/exp, cannot create \(x|v|^{1/3}\). **No match**.

### 3
Same issue as 2 (explicit \(+x\), log/exp removable, but no Abs power term). **No match**.

Has \(x v^{c4}\) (no Abs), plus log/exp removable, plus \(c2 x\). Cannot form \(x|v|^{1/3}\). **No match**.

### Core obstruction across all candidates
GT contains the essential non-analytic term \(x|v|^{1/3}\) (fractional power of absolute value). None of the candidates provide an \(x\cdot |v|^{c}\) term with a free exponent; they only offer:
- \(x|v|\) (power fixed at 1), or
- \(x v^{c}\) (no Abs), or
- \(x\log(1+a|v|)\), or
- \(x e^{a|v|}\), or
- polynomial-in-\(v\) times \(x\).

Because \(v\) can be negative, \(v^{1/3}\) (real cube root) is not equal to \(|v|^{1/3}\) for \(v<0\), and log/exp cannot equal a fractional power globally. Therefore no candidate can be made identical to the GT for all real \(v,x,t\).

[NO MATCH]

Conclusion: No match
